## <a name="microsoftcontainerregistry"></a><span data-ttu-id="7c0ce-1217">Microsoft.ContainerRegistry</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7c0ce-1217">Microsoft.ContainerRegistry</span></span>
